href="/wiki/Scripting_language" title="Scripting language">script</a> in the document. Also usable in the head and in block contexts.\n<dl><dd><em>Note:</em> <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;script&gt;</code> is not itself either a block or inline element; by itself it should not display at all, but it can contain instructions to dynamically generate either both block or inline content.</dd></dl></dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML32">HTML 3.2</a>; still current.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="sub"></span><span class="anchor" id="sub_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Subscript" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;sub</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/sub&gt;</b>\n</code> and <span class="anchor" id="sup"></span><span class="anchor" id="sup_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Superscript" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;sup</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/sup&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Mark <sub><a href="/wiki/Subscript" class="mw-redirect" title="Subscript">subscript</a></sub> or <sup><a href="/wiki/Superscript" class="mw-redirect" title="Superscript">superscript</a></sup> text. (Equivalent CSS: <code class="mw-highlight mw-highlight-lang-css mw-content-ltr" id="" style="" dir="ltr"><span class="p">{</span> <span class="k">vertical-align</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">sub</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="p">}</span></code> and <code class="mw-highlight mw-highlight-lang-css mw-content-ltr" id="" style="" dir="ltr"><span class="p">{</span> <span class="k">vertical-align</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="kc">super</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="p">}</span></code>, respectively.)</dd>\n<dd>Both were proposed in the <a href="#HTML30">HTML 3.0 Drafts</a>; <b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML32">HTML 3.2</a>; still current.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="template"></span><span class="anchor" id="template_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Template" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;template</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/template&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Code fragments to be copied by scripts.</dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML5">HTML5</a>.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="time"></span><span class="anchor" id="time_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Time" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;time</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/time&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Represents a time on the 24-hour clock or a date on the <a href="/wiki/Gregorian_calendar" title="Gregorian calendar">Gregorian calendar</a>, optionally with time and time zone information. Also allows times and dates to be represented in a machine-readable format.</dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML5">HTML5</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup></dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="wbr"></span><span class="anchor" id="wbr_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Word Break Opportunity" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;wbr</b><b style="color:#006633">&#160;/&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>An optional word break.</dd>\n<dd>Was widely used (and supported by all major browsers) for years despite being non-standard until finally being <b>standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML5">HTML5</a>.</dd></dl>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Images_and_objects">Images and objects</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=HTML_element&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Images and objects">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="applet"></span><span class="anchor" id="applet_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Java Applet" style="font-size:116%;"><del style="color:grey;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;applet</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/applet&gt;</b></del> <b>(deprecated)</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Embeds a <a href="/wiki/Java_applet" title="Java applet">Java applet</a> in the page. Deprecated in favor of <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;object&gt;</code>, as it could only be used with Java applets, and had accessibility limitations.</dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML32">HTML 3.2</a>; <b>deprecated</b> in <a href="#HTML401">HTML 4.0 Transitional</a>; <b>invalid</b> in <a href="#HTML401">HTML 4.0 Strict</a>. As of 2011, still widely used as the implementations of the replacing <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;object&gt;</code> are not consistent between different browsers.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="area"></span><span class="anchor" id="area_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Area" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;area</b><b style="color:#006633">&#160;/&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Specifies a <a href="/wiki/Focus_(computing)" title="Focus (computing)">focusable</a> area in a <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;map&gt;</code>.</dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML32">HTML 3.2</a>; still current.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="audio"></span><span class="anchor" id="audio_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Audio" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;audio</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/audio&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Adds playable <a href="/wiki/HTML5_audio" title="HTML5 audio">HTML5 audio</a> to the page. The audio URL is determined using the <code>src</code> attribute. Supported audio formats vary from browser to browser.</dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML5">HTML5</a>.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="canvas"></span><span class="anchor" id="canvas_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Canvas" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;canvas</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/canvas&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Canvas_element" title="Canvas element">Canvas element</a></div>\n<dl><dd>Adds a canvas whose contents can be edited with <a href="/wiki/JavaScript" title="JavaScript">JavaScript</a>. Frequently used for online games.</dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML5">HTML5</a>.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="embed"></span><code class="html" title="Embed" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;embed</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/embed&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Inserts a non-standard object (like applet) or external content (typically non-HTML) into the document. Deprecated in HTML 4 in favor of <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;object&gt;</code>, but then was added back into the HTML5 specification<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup></dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="img"></span><span class="anchor" id="img_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Image" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;img</b><b style="color:#006633">&#160;/&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Used by visual user agents to insert an <a href="/wiki/Image" title="Image">image</a> in the document. The <code>src</code> attribute specifies the image URL. The required <a href="/wiki/Alt_attribute" title="Alt attribute"><code>alt</code> attribute</a> provides alternative text in case the image cannot be displayed.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> (Though <code>alt</code> is intended as alternative text, Microsoft <a href="/wiki/Internet_Explorer" title="Internet Explorer">Internet Explorer</a> 7 and below render it as a <a href="/wiki/Tooltip" title="Tooltip">tooltip</a> if no <code>title</code> attribute is given.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Safari_(web_browser)" title="Safari (web browser)">Safari</a> and <a href="/wiki/Google_Chrome" title="Google Chrome">Google Chrome</a>, on the other hand, do not display the alt attribute at all.)<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup>  The <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;img&#32;&#47;&gt;</code> element was first proposed by <a href="/wiki/Marc_Andreessen" title="Marc Andreessen">Marc Andreessen</a> and implemented in the <a href="/wiki/Mosaic_(web_browser)" title="Mosaic (web browser)">NSCA Mosaic</a> web browser.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup></dd>\n<dd><code>IMG</code> existed in <i><a href="#HTMLDRAFT12">HTML Internet Draft 1.2</a></i>, and was <b>standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML20">HTML 2.0</a>; still current.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="map"></span><span class="anchor" id="map_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Image Map" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;map</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/map&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Specifies a client-side <a href="/wiki/Image_map" title="Image map">image map</a>.</dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML32">HTML 3.2</a>; still current.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="object"></span><span class="anchor" id="object_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Object" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;object</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/object&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Includes an <a href="/wiki/Media_Object" class="mw-redirect" title="Media Object">object</a> in the page of the type specified by the <code>type</code> attribute. This may be in any <a href="/wiki/MIME" title="MIME">MIME</a>-type the user agent understands, such as an embedded HTML page, a file to be handled by a plug-in such as <a href="/wiki/Macromedia_Flash" class="mw-redirect" title="Macromedia Flash">Flash</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Java_(programming_language)" title="Java (programming language)">Java</a> <a href="/wiki/Applet" title="Applet">applet</a>, a sound file, etc.</dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML401">HTML 4.0</a>; still current.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="param"></span><span class="anchor" id="param_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Object Parameter" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;param</b><b style="color:#006633">&#160;/&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Originally introduced with <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;applet&gt;</code>, this element is now used with <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;object&gt;</code>, and should only occur as a child of <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;object&gt;</code>. It uses <a href="/wiki/HTML_attributes" class="mw-redirect" title="HTML attributes">HTML attributes</a> to set a parameter for the object, e.g. width, height, font, background color, etc., depending on the type of object. An object can have multiple <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;param&#32;&#47;&gt;</code> elements.</dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML32">HTML 3.2</a>; still current.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="source"></span><span class="anchor" id="source_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Source" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;source</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/source&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Specifies different sources for audio or video. Makes use of the <code>src</code> attribute in a way similar to the <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;video&gt;</code> and <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;audio&gt;</code> elements.</dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML5">HTML5</a>.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="track"></span><span class="anchor" id="track_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Track" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;track</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/track&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Provides text tracks, like subtitles and captions, for audio and video.</dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML5">HTML5</a>.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="video"></span><span class="anchor" id="video_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Video" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;video</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/video&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Adds a playable <a href="/wiki/HTML5_video" title="HTML5 video">HTML5 video</a> to the page. The video URL is determined using the <code>src</code> attribute. Supported video formats vary from browser to browser.</dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML5">HTML5</a>.</dd></dl>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Forms">Forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=HTML_element&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Forms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Form_(HTML)" title="Form (HTML)">Form (HTML)</a></div>\n<p>These elements can be combined into a form or in some instances used separately as user-interface controls; in the document, they can be simple HTML or used in conjunction with Scripts. HTML markup specifies the elements that make up a form, and the method by which it will be submitted. However, some form of scripts (<a href="/wiki/Server-side_script" class="mw-redirect" title="Server-side script">server-side</a>, client-side, or both) must be used to process the user\'s input once it is submitted.\n</p><p>(These elements are either block or inline elements, but are collected here as their use is more restricted than other inline or block elements.)\n</p><p><span class="anchor" id="form"></span><span class="anchor" id="form_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Form" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;form</b><var style="color:#660066;" title="requiredAction&#160;(URL)"><b>&#160;action</b>="url"</var><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/form&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Creates a <a href="/wiki/Form_(web)" class="mw-redirect" title="Form (web)">form</a>. The <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;form&gt;</code> element specifies and operates the overall action of a form area, using the required <code>action</code> attribute.</dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML20">HTML 2.0</a>; still current.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="button"></span><span class="anchor" id="button_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Button" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;button</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/button&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>A generic form button which can contain a range of other elements to create complex buttons.</dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML401">HTML 4.0</a>; still current.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="datalist"></span><span class="anchor" id="datalist_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Data List" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;datalist</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/datalist&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>A list of <code>option</code>s for use in form elements.</dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML5">HTML5</a>.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="fieldset"></span><span class="anchor" id="fieldset_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Fieldset" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;fieldset</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/fieldset&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>A container for adding structure to forms. For example, a series of related controls can be grouped within a <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;fieldset&gt;</code>, which can then have a <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;legend&gt;</code> added in order to identify their function.</dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML401">HTML 4.0</a>; still current.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="input"></span><span class="anchor" id="input_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Input" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;input</b><b style="color:#006633">&#160;/&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd><code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;input&gt;</code> elements allow a variety of standard form controls to be implemented.</dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML20">HTML 2.0</a>; still current.</dd></dl>\n<dl><dd><b>Input Types:</b></dd>\n<dd><var style="color:#660066;" title="impliedField Type&#160;(ENUM)"><b>&#160;type</b>="checkbox"</var>\n<dl><dd>A <b><a href="/wiki/Checkbox" title="Checkbox">checkbox</a></b>. Can be checked or unchecked.</dd></dl></dd></dl>\n<dl><dd><var style="color:#660066;" title="impliedField Type&#160;(ENUM)"><b>&#160;type</b>="radio"</var>\n<dl><dd>A <b><a href="/wiki/Radio_button" title="Radio button">radio button</a></b>. If multiple radio buttons are given the same name, the user will only be able to select one of them from this group.</dd></dl></dd></dl>\n<dl><dd><var style="color:#660066;" title="impliedField Type&#160;(ENUM)"><b>&#160;type</b>="button"</var>\n<dl><dd>A general-purpose button. The element <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;button&gt;</code> is preferred if possible (i.e., if the client supports it) as it provides richer possibilities.</dd></dl></dd></dl>\n<dl><dd><var style="color:#660066;" title="impliedField Type&#160;(ENUM)"><b>&#160;type</b>="submit"</var>\n<dl><dd>A <b>submit</b> button.</dd></dl></dd></dl>\n<dl><dd><var style="color:#660066;" title="impliedField Type&#160;(ENUM)"><b>&#160;type</b>="image"</var>\n<dl><dd>An <b>image button</b>. The image URL may be specified with the <code>src</code> attribute.</dd></dl></dd></dl>\n<dl><dd><var style="color:#660066;" title="impliedField Type&#160;(ENUM)"><b>&#160;type</b>="reset"</var>\n<dl><dd>A <b>reset button</b> for resetting the form to default values.</dd></dl></dd></dl>\n<dl><dd><var style="color:#660066;" title="optionalField Type&#160;(ENUM)"><b>&#160;type</b>="text"</var>\n<dl><dd>A <b>one-line text input field</b>. The <code>size</code> attribute specifies the default width of the input in character-widths. <code>max-length</code> sets the maximum number of characters the user can enter (which may be greater than size).</dd></dl></dd></dl>\n<dl><dd><var style="color:#660066;" title="impliedField Type&#160;(ENUM)"><b>&#160;type</b>="search"</var>\n<dl><dd>A variation of <code>text</code> which produces a search bar.</dd></dl></dd></dl>\n<dl><dd><var style="color:#660066;" title="impliedField Type&#160;(ENUM)"><b>&#160;type</b>="password"</var>\n<dl><dd>A variation of <code>text</code>. The difference is that text typed in this field is <em>masked</em> \xe2\x80\x93 characters are displayed as an asterisk, a dot, or another replacement. The password is still submitted to the server as <a href="/wiki/Plaintext" title="Plaintext">plaintext</a>, so an underlying secure <a href="/wiki/Communication_protocol" title="Communication protocol">communication protocol</a> like <a href="/wiki/HTTPS" title="HTTPS">HTTPS</a> is needed if confidentiality is a concern.</dd></dl></dd></dl>\n<dl><dd><var style="color:#660066;" title="impliedField Type&#160;(ENUM)"><b>&#160;type</b>="file"</var>\n<dl><dd>A <a href="/wiki/File_select" title="File select">file select</a> field (for uploading files to a server).</dd></dl></dd></dl>\n<dl><dd><var style="color:#660066;" title="impliedField Type&#160;(ENUM)"><b>&#160;type</b>="tel"</var>\n<dl><dd>A variation of <code>text</code> for <a href="/wiki/Telephone_numbers" class="mw-redirect" title="Telephone numbers">telephone numbers</a>.</dd></dl></dd></dl>\n<dl><dd><var style="color:#660066;" title="impliedField Type&#160;(ENUM)"><b>&#160;type</b>="email"</var>\n<dl><dd>A variation of <code>text</code> for <a href="/wiki/Email_addresses" class="mw-redirect" title="Email addresses">email addresses</a>.</dd></dl></dd></dl>\n<dl><dd><var style="color:#660066;" title="impliedField Type&#160;(ENUM)"><b>&#160;type</b>="url"</var>\n<dl><dd>A variation of <code>text</code> for <a href="/wiki/URLs" class="mw-redirect" title="URLs">URLs</a>.</dd></dl></dd></dl>\n<dl><dd><var style="color:#660066;" title="impliedField Type&#160;(ENUM)"><b>&#160;type</b>="date"</var>\n<dl><dd>A date selector.</dd></dl></dd></dl>\n<dl><dd><var style="color:#660066;" title="impliedField Type&#160;(ENUM)"><b>&#160;type</b>="time"</var>\n<dl><dd>A time selector.</dd></dl></dd></dl>\n<dl><dd><var style="color:#660066;" title="impliedField Type&#160;(ENUM)"><b>&#160;type</b>="number"</var>\n<dl><dd>A variation of <code>text</code> for numbers.</dd></dl></dd></dl>\n<dl><dd><var style="color:#660066;" title="impliedField Type&#160;(ENUM)"><b>&#160;type</b>="range"</var>\n<dl><dd>Produces a slider for that returns a number, but the number is not visible to the user.</dd></dl></dd></dl>\n<dl><dd><var style="color:#660066;" title="impliedField Type&#160;(ENUM)"><b>&#160;type</b>="color"</var>\n<dl><dd>A color picker.</dd></dl></dd></dl>\n<dl><dd><var style="color:#660066;" title="impliedField Type&#160;(ENUM)"><b>&#160;type</b>="hidden"</var>\n<dl><dd><code>hidden</code> inputs are not visible in the rendered page, but allow a designer to maintain a copy of data that needs to be submitted to the server as part of the form. This may, for example, be data that this web user entered or selected on a previous form that needs to be processed in conjunction with the current form. Not displayed to the user but data can still be altered client-side by editing the HTML source.</dd></dl></dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="isindex"></span><span class="anchor" id="isindex_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Index" style="font-size:116%;"><del style="color:grey;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;isindex</b><b style="color:#006633">&#160;/&gt;</b></del> <b>(deprecated)</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd><code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;isindex&#32;&#47;&gt;</code> could either appear in the document head or in the body, but only once in a document.</dd>\n<dd><code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;isindex&#32;&#47;&gt;</code> operated as a primitive HTML search form; but was <i lang="la" title="Latin-language text"><a href="/wiki/De_facto" title="De facto">de facto</a></i> obsoleted by more advanced HTML forms introduced in the early to mid-1990s. Represents a set of hyperlinks composed of a base URI, an <a href="/wiki/Ampersand" title="Ampersand">ampersand</a> and <a href="/wiki/Percent-encoding" title="Percent-encoding">percent-encoded</a> keywords separated by <a href="/wiki/Plus_sign" class="mw-redirect" title="Plus sign">plus signs</a>.</dd>\n<dd><code>ISINDEX</code> existed in <i><a href="#HTMLTAGS">HTML Tags</a></i>; <b>standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML20">HTML 2.0</a>; <b>deprecated</b> in <a href="#HTML401">HTML 4.0 Transitional</a>; <b>invalid</b> in <a href="#HTML401">HTML 4.0 Strict</a>.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="keygen"></span><span class="anchor" id="keygen_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Key pair generator" style="font-size:116%;"><del style="color:grey;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;keygen</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/keygen&gt;</b></del> <b>(deprecated)</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>A key pair generator.</dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML5">HTML5</a>, but removed in HTML 5.2.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="label"></span><span class="anchor" id="label_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Label" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;label</b><var style="color:#660066;" title="impliedFor&#160;(ENUM)"><b>&#160;for</b>="id"</var><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/label&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Creates a label for a form input, such as <code>radio</code>. Clicking on the label fires a click on the matching input.</dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML401">HTML 4.0</a>; still current.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="legend"></span><span class="anchor" id="legend_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Legend" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;legend</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/legend&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>A legend (caption) for a <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;fieldset&gt;</code>.</dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML401">HTML 4.0</a>; still current.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="meter"></span><span class="anchor" id="meter_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Meter" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;meter</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/meter&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>A meter which needs a <code>value</code> attribute. Can also have: <code>min</code>, <code>low</code>, <code>high</code>, and <code>max</code>.</dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML5">HTML5</a>.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="option"></span><span class="anchor" id="option_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Select List Option" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;option</b><var style="color:#660066;" title="requiredValue&#160;(ANY)"><b>&#160;value</b>="x"</var><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/option&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Creates an item in a <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;select&gt;</code> list.</dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML20">HTML 2.0</a>; still current.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="optgroup"></span><span class="anchor" id="optgroup_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Options Group" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;optgroup</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/optgroup&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Identifies a group of <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;option&gt;</code> elements in a <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;select&gt;</code> list.</dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML401">HTML 4.0</a>; still current.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="output"></span><span class="anchor" id="output_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Output" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;output</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/output&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>The value of a form element.</dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML5">HTML5</a>.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="progress"></span><span class="anchor" id="progress_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Progress Bar" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;progress</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/progress&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>A bar for showing the progress of an action.</dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML5">HTML5</a>.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="select"></span><span class="anchor" id="select_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Selection List" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;select</b><var style="color:#660066;" title="impliedName&#160;(NMTOKEN)"><b>&#160;name</b>="xyz"</var><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/select&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Creates a selection list, from which the user can select a single option. May be rendered as a dropdown list.</dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML20">HTML 2.0</a>; still current.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="textarea"></span><span class="anchor" id="textarea_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Multiline Textarea" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;textarea</b><var style="color:#660066;" title="Rows&#160;(INT)"><b>&#160;rows</b>="8"</var><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/textarea&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>A multiple-line text area, the size of which is specified by <code>cols</code> (where a column is a one-character width of text) and <code>rows</code> <a href="/wiki/HTML_attributes" class="mw-redirect" title="HTML attributes">HTML attributes</a>. The content of this element is restricted to plain text, which appears in the text area as default text when the page is loaded.</dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML20">HTML 2.0</a>; still current.</dd></dl>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tables">Tables</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=HTML_element&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Tables">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The format of HTML Tables was proposed in the <a href="#HTML30">HTML 3.0 Drafts</a> and the later RFC 1942 <i><a href="#HTMLTABLES">HTML Tables</a></i>. They were inspired by the <a href="/wiki/CALS_Table_Model" title="CALS Table Model">CALS Table Model</a>. Some elements in these proposals were included in HTML 3.2; the present form of HTML Tables was standardized in HTML 4. (Many of the elements used within tables are neither <i>block</i> nor <i>inline</i> elements.)\n</p><p><span class="anchor" id="table"></span><span class="anchor" id="table_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Table" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;table</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/table&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Identifies a table. Several <a href="/wiki/HTML_attributes" class="mw-redirect" title="HTML attributes">HTML attributes</a> are possible in HTML Transitional, but most of these are invalid in HTML Strict and can be replaced with style sheets. The <code>summary</code> attribute is informally required for accessibility purposes, though its usage is not simple.</dd>\n<dd>Proposed in the <a href="#HTML30">HTML 3.0 Drafts</a>; <b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML32">HTML 3.2</a>; still current.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="tr"></span><span class="anchor" id="tr_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Table Row" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;tr</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/tr&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Contains a row of cells in a <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;table&gt;</code>.</dd>\n<dd>Proposed in the <a href="#HTML30">HTML 3.0 Drafts</a>; <b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML32">HTML 3.2</a>; still current.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="th"></span><span class="anchor" id="th_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Table Header Cell" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;th</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/th&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>A <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;table&gt;</code> header cell; contents are conventionally displayed bold and centered. An <a href="/wiki/Aural" class="mw-redirect" title="Aural">aural</a> user agent may use a louder voice for these items.</dd>\n<dd>Proposed in the <a href="#HTML30">HTML 3.0 Drafts</a>; <b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML32">HTML 3.2</a>; still current.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="td"></span><span class="anchor" id="td_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Table Data Cell" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;td</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/td&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>A <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;table&gt;</code> data cell.</dd>\n<dd>Proposed in the <a href="#HTML30">HTML 3.0 Drafts</a>; <b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML32">HTML 3.2</a>; still current.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="colgroup"></span><span class="anchor" id="colgroup_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Column Group" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;colgroup</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/colgroup&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Specifies a column group in a <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;table&gt;</code>.</dd>\n<dd>Proposed in <a href="#HTMLTABLES">HTML Tables</a>; <b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML401">HTML 4.0</a>; still current.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="col"></span><span class="anchor" id="col_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Table Column" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;col</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/col&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Specifies a column in a <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;table&gt;</code>.</dd>\n<dd>Proposed in <a href="#HTMLTABLES">HTML Tables</a>; <b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML401">HTML 4.0</a>; still current.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="caption"></span><span class="anchor" id="caption_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Table Caption" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;caption</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/caption&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Specifies a caption for a <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;table&gt;</code>.</dd>\n<dd>Proposed in the <a href="#HTML30">HTML 3.0 Drafts</a>; <b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML32">HTML 3.2</a>; still current.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="thead"></span><span class="anchor" id="thead_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Table Header" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;thead</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/thead&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Specifies the header part of a <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;table&gt;</code>. This section may be repeated by the user agent if the table is split across pages (in printing or other paged media).</dd>\n<dd>Proposed in <a href="#HTMLTABLES">HTML Tables</a>; <b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML401">HTML 4.0</a>; still current.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="tbody"></span><span class="anchor" id="tbody_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Table Body" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;tbody</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/tbody&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Specifies a body of data for a <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;table&gt;</code>.</dd>\n<dd>Proposed in <a href="#HTMLTABLES">HTML Tables</a>; <b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML401">HTML 4.0</a>; still current.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="tfoot"></span><span class="anchor" id="tfoot_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Table Footer" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;tfoot</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/tfoot&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Specifies the footer part of a <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;table&gt;</code>. Like <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;thead&gt;</code>, this section may be repeated by the user agent if the table is split across pages (in printing or other paged media).</dd>\n<dd>Proposed in <a href="#HTMLTABLES">HTML Tables</a>; <b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML401">HTML 4.0</a>; still current.</dd></dl>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Frames">Frames</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=HTML_element&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Frames">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Framing_(World_Wide_Web)" class="mw-redirect" title="Framing (World Wide Web)">Framing (World Wide Web)</a></div>\n<p>Frames allow a visual HTML browser window to be split into segments, each of which can show a different document. This can lower bandwidth use, as repeating parts of a layout can be used in one frame, while variable content is displayed in another. This may come at a certain usability cost, especially in non-visual user agents,<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> due to separate and independent documents (or websites) being displayed adjacent to each other and being allowed to interact with the same parent window. Because of this cost, frames (excluding the <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;iframe&gt;</code> element) are only allowed in HTML 4.01 Frame-set. Iframes can also hold documents on different servers. In this case the interaction between windows is blocked by the browser. Sites like <a href="/wiki/Facebook" title="Facebook">Facebook</a> and <a href="/wiki/Twitter" title="Twitter">Twitter</a> use iframes to display content (plugins) on third party websites. Google <a href="/wiki/AdSense" class="mw-redirect" title="AdSense">AdSense</a> uses iframes to display banners on third party websites.\n</p><p>In HTML 4.01, a document may contain a <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;head&gt;</code> and a <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;body&gt;</code> <em>or</em> a <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;head&gt;</code> and a <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;frameset&gt;</code>, but not both a <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;body&gt;</code> and a <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;frameset&gt;</code>. However, <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;iframe&gt;</code> can be used in a normal document body.\n</p><p><span class="anchor" id="frameset"></span><span class="anchor" id="frameset_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Frameset" style="font-size:116%;"><del style="color:grey;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;frameset</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/frameset&gt;</b></del> <b>(deprecated)</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Contains the set of <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;frame&#32;&#47;&gt;</code> elements for a document. The layout of frames is given by comma separated lists in the <code>rows</code> and <code>cols</code> <a href="/wiki/HTML_attributes" class="mw-redirect" title="HTML attributes">HTML attributes</a>.</dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML401">HTML 4.0</a> Frameset, <b>obsolete</b> in HTML5.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="frame"></span><span class="anchor" id="frame_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Frame" style="font-size:116%;"><del style="color:grey;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;frame</b><b style="color:#006633">&#160;/&gt;</b></del> <b>(deprecated)</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Defines a single frame, or region, within the <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;frameset&gt;</code>. A separate document is linked to a frame using the <code>src</code> attribute inside the <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;frame&#32;&#47;&gt;</code> element.</dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML401">HTML 4.0</a> Frameset, <b>obsolete</b> in HTML5.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="noframes"></span><span class="anchor" id="noframes_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Frame Support Fallback" style="font-size:116%;"><del style="color:grey;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;noframes</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/noframes&gt;</b></del> <b>(deprecated)</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Contains normal HTML content for user agents that don\'t support <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;frame&#32;&#47;&gt;</code> elements.</dd>\n<dd><b>Standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML401">HTML 4.0</a> Transitional, <b>obsolete</b> in HTML5.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="iframe"></span><span class="anchor" id="iframe_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Inline Frame" style="font-size:116%;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;iframe</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/iframe&gt;</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>An inline frame places another HTML document in a frame. Unlike an <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;object&#32;&#47;&gt;</code> element, an <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;iframe&gt;</code> can be the "target" frame for links defined by other elements, and it can be selected by the user agent as the focus for printing, viewing its source, and so on.</dd>\n<dd>The content of the element is used as alternative text to be displayed if the browser does not support inline frames.</dd>\n<dd>First introduced by Microsoft Internet Explorer in 1997, <b>standardized</b> in <a href="#HTML401">HTML 4.0</a> Transitional, <b>allowed</b> in HTML5.</dd></dl>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="longdesc_attribute"><code>longdesc</code> attribute</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=HTML_element&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: longdesc attribute">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>In <a href="/wiki/HTML" title="HTML">HTML</a>, <b><code>longdesc</code></b> is an attribute used within the <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;img&#32;&#47;&gt;</code>, <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;frame&#32;&#47;&gt;</code>, or <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;iframe&gt;</code> elements. It is supposed to be a <a href="/wiki/URL" title="URL">URL</a><sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;note 8&#93;</a></sup> to a document that provides a <b>long description</b> for the image, frame, or iframe in question.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> Note that this attribute should contain a URL, <em>not</em> \xe2\x80\x93 as is commonly mistaken \xe2\x80\x93 the text of the description itself.\n</p><p><code>longdesc</code> was designed to be used by <a href="/wiki/Screen_reader" title="Screen reader">screen readers</a> to display image information for computer users with <a href="/wiki/Accessibility" title="Accessibility">accessibility</a> issues, such as the blind or visually impaired, and is widely implemented by both web browsers and screen readers.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup>  Some developers object that<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> it is actually seldom used for this purpose because there are relatively few authors who use the attribute and most of those authors use it incorrectly; thus, they recommend deprecating <code>longdesc</code>.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> The publishing industry has responded, advocating the retention of <code>longdesc</code>.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Example">Example</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=HTML_element&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Example">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<div class="mw-highlight mw-highlight-lang-html mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"><pre><span></span><span class="p">&lt;</span><span class="nt">img</span> <span class="na">src</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s">&quot;Hello.jpg&quot;</span> <span class="na">longdesc</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s">&quot;description.html&quot;</span><span class="p">&gt;</span>\n</pre></div>\n<p><br />Content of <code>description.html</code>:\n</p>\n<div class="mw-highlight mw-highlight-lang-html mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"><pre><span></span><span class="p">&lt;</span><span class="nt">br</span> <span class="p">/&gt;</span>\n<span class="p">&lt;</span><span class="nt">p</span><span class="p">&gt;</span>This is an image of a two-layered birthday cake.<span class="p">&lt;/</span><span class="nt">p</span><span class="p">&gt;</span>\n...\n</pre></div>\n<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Linking_to_the_long_description_in_the_text">Linking to the long description in the text</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=HTML_element&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Linking to the long description in the text">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<p>Since very few graphical browsers support making the link available natively (Opera and iCab being the exceptions), it is useful to include a link to the description page near the <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;img&#32;&#47;&gt;</code> element whenever possible, as this can also aid sighted users.\n</p>\n<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Example_2">Example</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=HTML_element&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Example">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>\n<div class="mw-highlight mw-highlight-lang-html mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"><pre><span></span><span class="p">&lt;</span><span class="nt">img</span> <span class="na">src</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s">&quot;Hello.jpg&quot;</span> <span class="na">longdesc</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s">&quot;description.html&quot;</span> <span class="p">/&gt;</span> [<span class="p">&lt;</span><span class="nt">a</span> <span class="na">href</span><span class="o">=</span>\n<span class="s">&quot;description.html&quot;</span> <span class="na">title</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s">&quot;long description of the image&quot;</span><span class="p">&gt;</span>D<span class="p">&lt;/</span><span class="nt">a</span><span class="p">&gt;</span>]\n</pre></div>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Historic_elements">Historic elements</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=HTML_element&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Historic elements">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Comparison_of_layout_engines_(Non-standard_HTML)" class="mw-redirect" title="Comparison of layout engines (Non-standard HTML)">Comparison of layout engines (Non-standard HTML)</a></div>\n<p>The following elements were part of the early HTML developed by <a href="/wiki/Tim_Berners-Lee" title="Tim Berners-Lee">Tim Berners-Lee</a> from 1989 to 1991; they are mentioned in <i>HTML Tags</i>, but deprecated in <i>HTML 2.0</i> and were never part of HTML standards.\n</p><p><span class="anchor" id="listing"></span><span class="anchor" id="listing_tag"></span><code class="html" title="HTML Listing" style="font-size:116%;"><del style="color:grey;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;listing</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/listing&gt;</b></del> <b>(deprecated)</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>This element displayed the text inside the tags in a monospace font and without interpreting the HTML. The <a href="#HTML20">HTML 2.0</a> specification recommended rendering the element at up to 132 characters per line.</dd>\n<dd><b>Deprecated</b> in <a href="#HTML32">HTML 3.2</a>; <b>obsolete</b> in <a href="#HTML5">HTML5</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup></dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="plaintext"></span><span class="anchor" id="plaintext_tag"></span><code class="html" title="Plaintext" style="font-size:116%;"><del style="color:grey;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;plaintext</b><b style="color:#006633">&#160;/&gt;</b></del> <b>(deprecated)</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd><code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;plaintext&#32;&#47;&gt;</code> does not have an end tag as it terminates the markup and causes the rest of the document to be parsed as if it were <a href="/wiki/Plaintext" title="Plaintext">plaintext</a>.</dd>\n<dd><code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;plaintext&#32;&#47;&gt;</code> existed in <i><a href="#HTMLTAGS">HTML Tags</a></i>; <b>deprecated</b> in <a href="#HTML20">HTML 2.0</a>; <b>invalid</b> in <a href="#HTML401">HTML 4.0</a>.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="xmp"></span><span class="anchor" id="xmp_tag"></span><code class="html" title="HTML Example" style="font-size:116%;"><del style="color:grey;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;xmp</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/xmp&gt;</b></del> <b>(deprecated)</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>This element displayed the text inside the tags in a monospace font and without interpreting the HTML. The <a href="#HTML20">HTML 2.0</a> specification recommended rendering the element at 80 characters per line.</dd>\n<dd><b>Deprecated</b> in <a href="#HTML32">HTML 3.2</a>; <b>obsolete</b> in <a href="#HTML5">HTML5</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup></dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="nextid"></span><span class="anchor" id="nextid_tag"></span><code class="html" title="NeXT ID" style="font-size:116%;"><del style="color:grey;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;nextid</b><b style="color:#006633">&#160;/&gt;</b></del> <b>(deprecated)</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>This element enabled NeXT web designing tool to generate automatic NAME labels for its anchors and was itself automatically generated.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup></dd>\n<dd><code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;nextid&#32;&#47;&gt;</code> existed in <i><a href="#HTMLTAGS">HTML Tags</a></i> (described as obsolete); <b>deprecated</b> in <a href="#HTML20">HTML 2.0</a>; <b>invalid</b> in <a href="#HTML32">HTML 3.2</a> and later.</dd></dl>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Non-standard_elements">Non-standard elements</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=HTML_element&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Non-standard elements">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Comparison_of_layout_engines_(Non-standard_HTML)" class="mw-redirect" title="Comparison of layout engines (Non-standard HTML)">Comparison of layout engines (Non-standard HTML)</a></div>\n<p>This section lists some widely used obsolete elements, which means they are not used in <a href="/wiki/Validator" title="Validator">valid</a> code. They may not be supported in all user agents.\n</p><p><span class="anchor" id="blink"></span><code class="html" title="Blink" style="font-size:116%;"><del style="color:grey;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;blink</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/blink&gt;</b></del> <b>(deprecated)</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Blink_element" title="Blink element">Blink element</a></div>\n<dl><dd>Causes text to blink. Introduced in imitation of the <a href="/wiki/ANSI_escape_code" title="ANSI escape code">ANSI escape codes</a>. Can be done with CSS where supported: <code class="mw-highlight mw-highlight-lang-css mw-content-ltr" id="" style="" dir="ltr"><span class="p">{</span><span class="k">text-decoration</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="kc">blink</span><span class="p">}</span></code> (This effect may have negative consequences for people with <a href="/wiki/Photosensitive_epilepsy" title="Photosensitive epilepsy">photosensitive epilepsy</a>;<sup id="cite_ref-WCAG_71-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WCAG-71">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> its use on the public Internet should follow the appropriate guidelines.)</dd>\n<dd><code class="mw-highlight mw-highlight-lang-html mw-content-ltr" id="" style="" dir="ltr"><span class="p">&lt;</span><span class="nt">blink</span><span class="p">&gt;</span></code> originated in <a href="/wiki/Netscape_Navigator" title="Netscape Navigator">Netscape Navigator</a> and is mostly recognized by its descendants, including <a href="/wiki/Firefox" title="Firefox">Firefox</a>; <b>deprecated</b> or <b>invalid</b> in <a href="#HTML20">HTML 2.0</a> and later. Note that the replacement CSS tag, while standard, is not required to be supported.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="layer"></span><code class="html" title="Layer" style="font-size:116%;"><del style="color:grey;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;layer</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/layer&gt;</b></del> <b>(deprecated)</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Layer_element" title="Layer element">Layer element</a></div>\n<dl><dd>Creates an absolute positioned and framed layer. Can be done with frames and/or CSS instead. There are attributes, including <b>ID</b>, <b>LEFT</b>, <b>TOP</b>, <b>PAGEX</b>, <b>PAGEY</b>, <b>SRC</b>, <b>Z-INDEX</b>, <b>ABOVE</b>, <b>WIDTH</b>, <b>HEIGHT</b>, <b>BELOW</b>, <b>CLIP</b>, <b>VISIBILITY</b> and <b>CLIP</b>.</dd>\n<dd><code class="mw-highlight mw-highlight-lang-html mw-content-ltr" id="" style="" dir="ltr"><span class="p">&lt;</span><span class="nt">layer</span><span class="p">&gt;</span></code> originated in <a href="/wiki/Netscape_4" class="mw-redirect" title="Netscape 4">Netscape 4</a>; <b>deprecated</b> or <b>invalid</b> in <a href="#HTML401">HTML 4.01</a> and later.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="marquee"></span><code class="html" title="Marquee" style="font-size:116%;"><del style="color:grey;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;marquee</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/marquee&gt;</b></del> <b>(deprecated)</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Marquee_element" title="Marquee element">Marquee element</a></div>\n<dl><dd>Creates scrolling text. Can be done with scripting instead. (This effect may have negative consequences for people with <a href="/wiki/Photosensitive_epilepsy" title="Photosensitive epilepsy">photosensitive epilepsy</a>;<sup id="cite_ref-WCAG_71-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WCAG-71">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> its use on the public Internet should follow the appropriate guidelines.) There are three options, including <b>Alternate</b>, <b>Scroll</b> and <b>slide</b>. <b>Scrolldelay</b> can also be added.</dd>\n<dd><code class="mw-highlight mw-highlight-lang-html mw-content-ltr" id="" style="" dir="ltr"><span class="p">&lt;</span><span class="nt">marquee</span><span class="p">&gt;</span></code> originated in <a href="/wiki/Microsoft_Internet_Explorer" class="mw-redirect" title="Microsoft Internet Explorer">Microsoft Internet Explorer</a>; <b>deprecated</b> or <b>invalid</b> in <a href="#HTML401">HTML 4.01</a> and later.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="nobr"></span><code class="html" title="No Break" style="font-size:116%;"><del style="color:grey;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;nobr</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/nobr&gt;</b></del> <b>(deprecated)</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Causes text to not break at end of line, preventing word wrap where text exceeds the width of the enclosing object. Adjacent text may break before and after it. Can be done with CSS: <code class="mw-highlight mw-highlight-lang-css mw-content-ltr" id="" style="" dir="ltr"><span class="p">{</span><span class="k">white-space</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="kc">nowrap</span><span class="p">;}</span></code></dd>\n<dd><code class="mw-highlight mw-highlight-lang-html mw-content-ltr" id="" style="" dir="ltr"><span class="p">&lt;</span><span class="nt">nobr</span><span class="p">&gt;</span></code> is a proprietary element which is recognized by most browsers for compatibility reasons; <b>deprecated</b> or <b>invalid</b> in <a href="#HTML20">HTML 2.0</a> and later.</dd></dl>\n<p><span class="anchor" id="noembed"></span><code class="html" title="Embed Fallback" style="font-size:116%;"><del style="color:grey;"><b style="color:#006633">&lt;noembed</b><b style="color:#006633">&gt;</b>...<b style="color:#006633">&lt;/noembed&gt;</b></del> <b>(deprecated)</b>\n</code>\n</p>\n<dl><dd>Specifies alternative content, if the embed cannot be rendered. Replaced by the content of the <code class="mw-highlight mw-highlight-lang-html mw-content-ltr" id="" style="" dir="ltr"><span class="p">&lt;</span><span class="nt">embed</span><span class="p">&gt;</span></code> or <code class="mw-highlight mw-highlight-lang-html mw-content-ltr" id="" style="" dir="ltr"><span class="p">&lt;</span><span class="nt">object</span><span class="p">&gt;</span></code> element.</dd></dl>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Comments">Comments</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=HTML_element&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Comments">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<dl><dt><code class="mw-highlight mw-highlight-lang-html mw-content-ltr" id="" style="" dir="ltr"><span class="c">&lt;!-- A Comment --&gt;</span></code></dt></dl>\n<p><br />A <a href="/wiki/Comment_(computer_programming)" title="Comment (computer programming)">comment</a> in HTML (and related XML, SGML and SHTML) uses the same syntax as the <a href="/wiki/SGML_comment" class="mw-redirect" title="SGML comment">SGML comment</a> or <a href="/wiki/XML_comment" class="mw-redirect" title="XML comment">XML comment</a>, depending on the doctype.\n</p><p>Unlike most HTML tags, comments do not nest.\n</p><p>The markup <code class="mw-highlight mw-highlight-lang-html mw-content-ltr" id="" style="" dir="ltr"><span class="c">&lt;!--Xbegin&lt;!--Y--&gt;</span>Xend--&gt;</code> will yield the comment <samp style="padding-left:0.4em; padding-right:0.4em; color:#666666;"><span class="nowrap">Xbegin&lt;!--Y</span></samp> and the text <samp style="padding-left:0.4em; padding-right:0.4em; color:#666666;"><span class="nowrap">Xend--&gt;</span></samp> after it, or sometimes just <samp style="padding-left:0.4em; padding-right:0.4em; color:#666666;">Xend--&gt;</samp>, depending on browser.\n</p><p>Comments can appear anywhere in a document, as the HTML parser is supposed to ignore them no matter where they appear so long as they are not inside other HTML tag structures (i.e., they cannot be used next to attributes and values; this is invalid markup: <code><span class="nowrap">&lt;span id="x1"</span><span class="nowrap">&lt;--for</span> "extension <span class="nowrap">one"--&gt;</span> <span class="nowrap">style="..."&lt;</span></code>).\n</p><p>Comments can even appear before the doctype declaration; no other tags are permitted to do this.\n</p><p>However, not all browsers and HTML editors are fully compliant with the HTML syntax framework and may do unpredictable things under some syntax conditions. Defective handling of comments only affects about 5% of all browsers and HTML editors in use, and even then only certain versions are affected by comment mishandling issues (Internet Explorer 6 accounts for most of this high percentage).\n</p><p>There are a few compatibility quirks involving comments:\n</p>\n<ul><li>Placing comments \xe2\x80\x93 or indeed any characters except for white-space \xe2\x80\x93 before the <code>doctype</code> will cause Internet Explorer 6 to use <a href="/wiki/Quirks_mode" title="Quirks mode">quirks mode</a> for the HTML page. None of the <code>doctype</code> information will be processed.</li>\n<li>For compatibility with some pre-1995 browsers, the contents of <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;style&gt;</code> and <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;script&gt;</code> elements are still sometimes surrounded by comment delimiters, and CSS- and script-capable browsers are written to specifically ignore that comment markup as not actually a comment. This means that attempts to actually comment out CSS and script markup by change the elements inside the comment to not be recognized, e.g. <code><span class="nowrap">&lt;--</span> <span class="nowrap">[script]...</span>[/script] <span class="nowrap">--&gt;</span></code>.</li>\n<li>The <a href="/wiki/BlueGriffon" title="BlueGriffon">BlueGriffon</a> HTML editor, in versions 1.7.<var style="padding-right: 1px;">x</var>, makes comments that are not embedded in the syntax structure; <code class="mw-highlight mw-highlight-lang-html mw-content-ltr" id="" style="" dir="ltr"><span class="p">&lt;</span><span class="nt">style</span><span class="p">&gt;</span> <span class="o">...</span> <span class="p">{</span><span class="err">comment</span> <span class="err">tags</span><span class="p">}</span> <span class="o">...</span><span class="p">&lt;/</span><span class="nt">style</span><span class="p">&gt;</span></code> will show up on-screen. Other HTML editors may have this same defect.</li></ul>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">See also</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=HTML_element&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: See also">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/HTML_attribute" title="HTML attribute">HTML attribute</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/HTML#Element_examples" title="HTML">HTML element examples</a></li></ul>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes">Notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=HTML_element&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1011085734">.mw-parser-output .reflist{font-size:90%;margin-bottom:0.5em;list-style-type:decimal}.mw-parser-output .reflist .references{font-size:100%;margin-bottom:0;list-style-type:inherit}.mw-parser-output .reflist-columns-2{column-width:30em}.mw-parser-output .reflist-columns-3{column-width:25em}.mw-parser-output .reflist-columns{margin-top:0.3em}.mw-parser-output .reflist-columns ol{margin-top:0}.mw-parser-output .reflist-columns li{page-break-inside:avoid;break-inside:avoid-column}.mw-parser-output .reflist-upper-alpha{list-style-type:upper-alpha}.mw-parser-output .reflist-upper-roman{list-style-type:upper-roman}.mw-parser-output .reflist-lower-alpha{list-style-type:lower-alpha}.mw-parser-output .reflist-lower-greek{list-style-type:lower-greek}.mw-parser-output .reflist-lower-roman{list-style-type:lower-roman}</style><div class="reflist" style="">\n<div class="mw-references-wrap"><ol class="references">\n<li id="cite_note-1"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-1">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">"Document" could be either a file stored on a computer <a href="/wiki/Filesystem" class="mw-redirect" title="Filesystem">filesystem</a> (usually on disk) or to an <a href="/wiki/HTTP" class="mw-redirect" title="HTTP">HTTP</a> delivery across the Web. The delivery could have been copied from the <a href="/wiki/Web_server" title="Web server">web server</a> or generated on demand.</span>\n</li>\n<li id="cite_note-4"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-4">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="/wiki/Document_Object_Model" title="Document Object Model">Document Object Model</a> is now a formalized specification by the <a href="/wiki/W3C" class="mw-redirect" title="W3C">W3C</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-W3C_Current_DOM_version_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-W3C_Current_DOM_version-2">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> It defines <em>an interface to</em> this internal model, rather than the internal model itself. Early web browsers used their own internal representation that bore little relation to the DOM. The term "document tree" has also been applied.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> However for the purpose here, of explaining the difference between a document and a parsed model, it is convenient to use the term DOM throughout.</span>\n</li>\n<li id="cite_note-5"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-5">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The term "web browser" here is used for simplicity. It does of course include other sorts of <a href="/wiki/Web_user_agent" class="mw-redirect" title="Web user agent">web user agent</a>, such as search engine <a href="/wiki/Web_crawler" title="Web crawler">web crawlers</a>, automatic news-feed retrievers etc.</span>\n</li>\n<li id="cite_note-9"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-9">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">HTML 4.01 is one of a small number of well-known HTML DTDs. It is chosen here as the best illustrative example, although the same behavior applies to the other W3C-published DTDs for HTML.</span>\n</li>\n<li id="cite_note-11"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-11">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">A macro-like feature of DTDs may still be used within XML.</span>\n</li>\n<li id="cite_note-13"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-13">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">One minor difference is that XML, even after the DOM interface, is case-sensitive.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup></span>\n</li>\n<li id="cite_note-15"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-15">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">However, see <code class="mw-highlight mw-highlight-lang-html mw-content-ltr" id="" style="" dir="ltr"><span class="p">&lt;</span><span class="nt">object</span><span class="p">&gt;</span></code> for the inevitable exception.</span>\n</li>\n<li id="cite_note-62"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-62">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Strictly an <a href="/wiki/Internationalized_resource_identifier" class="mw-redirect" title="Internationalized resource identifier">IRI</a>, not a URL; although URLs are a subset of IRIs.</span>\n</li>\n</ol></div></div>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="References">References</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a
